name:S‚Äçu‚Äçn‚Äçz‚Äçh‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçl‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçg

posted:Posted May 26, 2024
msg:"Wanda Meihua Resort Hotel Xitang" is located at No. 325, North Huanzhen Road, Xitang Town, and is only one bridge away from "Xitang Ancient Town", one of the top ten ancient towns in China. The hotel opened in October 2023, adopting the new Chinese Hui style of architecture, perfectly integrating blue bricks and white tiles with the environment of the ancient town.
The style of the hotel uses modern techniques to show the elements of the misty corridors and pavilions and ancient bridges in the Jiangnan water town, while using natural materials to coordinate with the natural environment to create a harmonious living a**osphere. (Details are taken from the Internet)
The style of "Huanxiu Elegant River View Room" combines traditional and modern design elements, with a simple style as the main style and soft color matching, creating a warm and peaceful a**osphere. The tent used for bedside decoration and the exquisite murals on the background wall add an artistic a**osphere to the room. The 1.8-meter bed is soft and comfortable, ensuring a good sleep experience after visiting the ancient town.
The hotel's breakfast restaurant has a spacious and bright dining environment, as well as a landscape seat and an outdoor dining area, so you can get closer to nature while enjoying breakfast. The meal fee of 68 yuan has a variety of Chinese and Western cuisines to choose from.
The hotel's gym is worth mentioning. It is the smallest gym among the hotels I have stayed in on four continents around the world. Although it has both strength and aerobics, it is at most a family gym.
The hotel's service is top-notch among resort hotels, providing guests with a full range of personalized service experience. Although it is a "front desk butler", it is not inferior to the "private butler" of some seven-star hotels, but it is better in some details. Especially the "good night milk" service, I was very moved. Special thanks to the butler "Jia Jia" for providing us with the best service of Wanda Huamei! ! !
Finally, I complain about XC. 2024 is already halfway through, and I can only share 30 seconds of videos... If you want to see the full version of the video I made, search for the same ID on other platforms on the 27th.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Elegant Room - River-View (2 Beds)
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted February 13, 2024
msg:The hotel is located by the water, 100 meters away from the entrance of Wolong Bridge in Xitang Ancient Town, with an excellent location. 
The check-in time of the hotel is generally long in the middle of the year. I didn't expect to receive a call from Xiao Wu, the hotel customer service, at noon to confirm the arrival time with me. I prepared in advance and checked in immediately after arriving. Thank you~
The ticket price agreed by the scenic spot and the hotel is 70/person, and students under 18 years old can buy tickets on site at half price of 45. They can enter and exit freely within two days by face recognition, which is fast and convenient.
The underground parking garage of the hotel is equipped with charging piles, and the electricity fee is 2.75/kWh (including service fee), which is more expensive than the urban area and can be used for temporary emergency.
The breakfast place is not big, Chinese and Western food, drinks, desserts, and fruits are all available. Although the room is full, the meal is orderly and there is no feeling of crowding.
